msg:The hotel's hygiene was not good enough. I stayed at the Beijing JW Marriott Hotel from September 10th to September 12th. Before going to bed on the night of September 10th, I took the towel hanging in the bathroom to wipe my eyes and wash my face. 9 Between 8 a.m. and 10 a.m. on the 11th, I had an obvious foreign body sensation in my eyes. My friend who lived with me told me that my eyes were red and bloodshot. I didn‚Äôt care at the time and thought it might be me. It was caused by not getting a good rest. As a result, my eyes still didn‚Äôt get better the next day but got worse. I didn‚Äôt care about it, thinking that maybe I still didn‚Äôt have a good rest. Until the 14th, my eyes became worse day by day. The pain was unbearable and I felt like a foreign body. When I was strong, I decided to go to the hospital for a checkup. After the diagnosis and trea**ent, the doctor informed me that I had contracted ophthalmitis and it was very serious. I was prescribed relevant medicines. On the 15th, I returned to Hangzhou from Beijing. After 2 days The medication didn't make it any better, but made it worse, so I went to Shaw Hospital in Hangzhou for another check-up. The doctor told me that I was now infected with highly viral bacterial conjunctivitis, which was very serious. The illness is most likely caused by foreign objects coming into close contact with the eyeballs. I personally never have anything else come into contact with my eyes. The only time I concluded this was when I used a towel from the guest room facilities to wash my face and wipe my eyes in the JW Marriott Hotel room on the night of the 10th. As a result, it is not difficult to rule out that the previous guest had conjunctivitis and used this towel, but the hotel housekeeping depar**ent did not do a certain disinfection and cleaning before reusing the towel for the next guest, which led to my eye infection. This This disease is commonly known as pinkeye (highly contagious) and the pain is unbearable. I often stay in hotels and have never encountered such a situation. Now my eyes have not recovered and are getting worse. I hope the hotel will see this. When commenting on the message, actively correct and clean the guest room towels to prevent similar situations from happening and causing unnecessary trouble to other guests!
